    function followersIframeOpen(url) {
      gapi.load("gapi.iframes", function() {
        if (gapi.iframes &amp;&amp; gapi.iframes.getContext) {
          window.followersIframe = gapi.iframes.getContext().openChild({
            url: url,
            where: document.getElementById("followers-iframe-container"),
            messageHandlersFilter: gapi.iframes.CROSS_ORIGIN_IFRAMES_FILTER,
            messageHandlers: {
              '_ready': function(obj) {
                window.followersIframe.getIframeEl().height = obj.height;
              },
              'reset': function() {
                window.followersIframe.close();
                followersIframeOpen("https://www.blogger.com/followers.g?blogID\x3d5711314660374261745\x26origin\x3dhttp://www.unitedstatesofmotherhood.com/\x26colors\x3dCgt0cmFuc3BhcmVudBILdHJhbnNwYXJlbnQaBmZmZmZmZiIGM0Q4MUVFKgZmZmZmZmYyBmNjMDAwMDoGZmZmZmZmQgYzRDgxRUVKBmZmZmZjY1IGM0Q4MUVFWgt0cmFuc3BhcmVudA%3D%3D\x26postID\x3d8765051387779258775");

                followersIframeOpen(url);
              }
            }
          });
        }
      });

             <h3 class="post-title">
              <a href="http://www.unitedstatesofmotherhood.com/2012/08/giveaway-k-k-k-k-k-k-kia-gotta-give-it.html">
               Giveaway: K-k-k-k-k-k-kia!  Gotta Give it Up to the KIA Sorento!
              </a>
             </h3>
             <div class="post-header-line-1">
             </div>
             <div class="post-body">
              <p>
               <script language="JavaScript1.1" src="http://oascentral.blogher.org/RealMedia/ads/adstream_jx.ads/ReviewBadge/OID2752_Kia_Badge_005/@x13" type="text/javascript">

                Kia
               </a>
               !Woo hoo Kia? Hey baby! I lurve you!
               <br/>
               <br/>
              </p>

              <div style="text-align: center;">
               <b>
                What? You all want to know why?
               </b>
               <br/>
               <b>
                <br/>
               </b>
              </div>
              Well,
              <a href="http://goo.gl/sTkaV" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
               Kia
              </a>
              let me borrow their gorgeous Sorento for a week this month to review. When they dropped off this sparkly silver beauty, I just about fainted.
              <br/>
              <br/>
              <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
               <tbody>
                <tr>
                 <td style="text-align: center;">
                  <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-rIKWE-8xtas/UC0yiFGykkI/AAAAAAAAGaY/eKo63zwdALc/s1600/kia+18.jpg" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                   <img border="0" height="400" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-rIKWE-8xtas/UC0yiFGykkI/AAAAAAAAGaY/eKo63zwdALc/s400/kia+18.jpg" width="400"/>
                  </a>
                 </td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                 <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                  <span style="color: #666666;">
                   Sparkly and silver and better than glitter and unicorns
                  </span>
                 </td>
                </tr>
               </tbody>
              </table>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
              </div>
              No scratches. Clean windows, No smell of spoiled slushy of chocolate milk and ground goldfish crackers fermenting for the last nine years. Safety features out the wazoo. Bluetooth Wireless Technology for hands free talking to the hubs whilst driving to another play date? FULL gas tank!
              <br/>
              <br/>
              <div style="text-align: center;">
               <b>
                Yep, that was just the surface and it was already a busy swim/football mom and blogger's dream.
               </b>
               <br/>
               <b>
                <br/>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
              </div>
              <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
               <tbody>

                 <td style="text-align: center;">

                   <img border="0" height="400" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-OLcyTpE86Qg/UC0yVmRwKnI/AAAAAAAAGZQ/QcM7sDNUPZc/s400/kia+9.jpg" width="400"/>
                  </a>

              <br/>
              Oh baby. I was in heaven.
              <br/>
              <br/>
              <div style="text-align: center;">
               <b>
                Mine, mine, all mine for the week!
               </b>
               <br/>
               <b>
                <br/>
               </b>
              </div>
              Yes, Scout's Honor likes herself some
              <i>
               eau de new car
              </i>
              . Then there was the head rush when I got behind the wheel. I admit when I get rentals and reviews, I like to really TEST them.

              I revved. I rode those curves.

              <br/>
              I took bridges. We took ferries. We took corners. We searched out back-roads.We might have gone a smidge bit faster than I normally drive. People, I take reviewing seriously so I worked that baby out like it was a quarter horse in the Grand Canyon. It responded like a stud taking an afternoon stroll...with plenty of endurance (read fabulous gas mileage) to keep it coming.
              <br/>
              <br/>
              That was my take.
              <a href="http://goo.gl/sTkaV" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
               This crossover Kia
              </a>
              had the space of my SUV, but the response of a V-6 performance car and the gas mileage of a mini-van. Sooooo much fun. I am sold! We took curves....

                  <span style="text-align: justify;">
                   Kia told me that the Sorento, with advanced technology, sporty styling, and a spacious interior, was the first crossover that everyone will want to drive and starting at a little over $23,000, it's the crossover that makes the most sense to own.

                 <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                 </div>
                 <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                  <tbody>
                   <tr>
                    <td style="text-align: center;">
                     <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Kxi3q37dLK4/UC0yLcmxWgI/AAAAAAAAGYo/fDKwDFI32z0/s1600/kia+4.jpg" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                      <img border="0" height="400" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Kxi3q37dLK4/UC0yLcmxWgI/AAAAAAAAGYo/fDKwDFI32z0/s400/kia+4.jpg" width="400"/>
                     </a>
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                   <tr>
                    <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                     <span style="color: #666666;">
                      Sniffle! Bye, bye...for now!
                     </span>
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                  </tbody>
                 </table>
                 <div style="text-align: justify;">
                  <br/>
                  So my friends? Clearly being an ingrained California girl transplanted in Seattle, driving is my thing. My joy. My life as a mom. I was happy to try something new on for size. What about you?
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                 </div>
                 <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 </div>
                 <div style="text-align: justify;">
                  <b>
                   Tell me what feature of the Kia Sorento you would most enjoy and be entered for a chance to win an Asus Eee Pad Transformer Prime Android Tablet!!
                  </b>
                  <br/>
                  <b>
                   <br/>
                  </b>
                 </div>
                 <div style="text-align: justify;">
                  <b>
                   <br/>
                  </b>
                 </div>

                  <span style="color: #666666; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: x-small;">

                   a) Leave a comment in response to the sweepstakes prompt on this post
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="color: #666666; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: x-small;">
                   b) Tweet about this promotion (include #KiaSweepstakesEntry in your tweet) and leave the URL to that tweet in a comment on this post
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="color: #666666; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: x-small;">
                   c) Blog about this promotion on your own blog and leave the URL to that post in a comment on this post
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="color: #666666; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: x-small;">
                   d) For those with no Twitter or blog, read the official rules to learn about an alternate form of entry.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="color: #666666; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: x-small;">
                   Entries from all participating blogs will be pooled for winner selection; only two entries per household. This giveaway is open to US Residents age 18 or older. Winners will be selected via random draw, and will be notified by e-mail. You have 72 hours to get back to me, otherwise a new winner will be selected.
                  </span>

You know what I really like about Kia... it&#39;s that it&#39;s South Korean. Those awesome little people rose up (with our help) from oppressive tyranny and almost certain annihilation from the communist regime in the North. Kia went from making steel tubes by hand, to bicycles to making military vehicles; to making commercial buses and pretty awesome consumer vehicles.
&lt;/p&gt;
